TITLE      Double differential neutron emission cross sections    12928  1    3 
           of 10B and 11B at 6, 10 and 14 MeV and of 6Li, 7Li     12928  1    4 
           and 12C at 14 MeV.                                     12928  1    5

           (C,85SANTA,1,145,198505) preliminary results.          12928  1    9 
REL-REF    (O,12986001,M.Drosg+,R,LA-10665-MS,1986)               12928  1   10 
            Data at 6 and 10 MeV                                  12928  1   11 
INSTITUTE  (1USALAS,2AUSVIE)                                      12928  1   12 
FACILITY   (VDGT,1USALAS) Vertical Van-de-Graaff.                 12928  1   13 
INC-SOURCE (D-T)                                                  12928  1   14 
PART-DET   (N)                                                    12928  1   15 
DETECTOR   (SCIN) Neutron detector (5.0 cm diameter x 2.5 cm      12928  1   16

MONIT-REF  ((MONIT),J.C.Hopkins+,J,ND/A,9,137,1971)               12928  1   20 
CORRECTION Corrected for multiple scattering. The data are NOT    12928  1   21 
           corrected for the finite angular resolution of         12928  1   22 
           typically +- 5 degree.                                 12928  1   23 
ERR-ANALYS The final error given with each data point of          12928  1   24 
           the secondary neutron spectra consists of the          12928  1   25 
           counting statistics of the individual spectra plus     12928  1   26 
           contributions of various corrections.                  12928  1   27 
           (ERR-1) Individual angle error.                        12928  1   28 
           (ERR-2,,1.)  Target mass error includes weight and     12928  1   29 
           purity.                                                12928  1   30 
           (ERR-3,,1.5) Monitor cross section.                    12928  1   31 
           (ERR-4,,0.5) Normalization: calibration of the         12928  1   32 
           experimental set-up using a detector with a given      12928  1   33 
           efficiency curve in a given geometry; it depends on the12928  1   34 
            evaluation of the monitor counts and the beam charge  12928  1   35 
           collection.                                            12928  1   36 
           (ERR-5) Geometry: difference in the positioning of the 12928  1   37 
           sample with regard to the neutron source and the       12928  1   38 
           detector; within one angular distribution this         12928  1   39 
           uncertainty is uncorrelated, but not for the reference 12928  1   40 
           measurement.                                           12928  1   41 
           (ERR-6) The Monte Carlo simulation corrects for flux   12928  1   42 
           attenuation,multiple scattering and finite sample size.12928  1   43 
           (ERR-S) consists of the combined statistical errors,   12928  1   44 
           the error in the deadtime correction and in the        12928  1   45 
           background subtraction.                                12928  1   46

ANALYSIS   (INTAD,INTED) The integration of the double            12928  2    6 
           differential cross section over both the energy of     12928  2    7 
           the emitted neutrons and the solid angle was done in   12928  2    8 
           two steps: first, the cross section of the highest     12928  2    9 
           energy peak was converted into the center-of-mass      12928  2   10 
           system, and then the remainder was integrated over     12928  2   11 
           the energy and the solid angle in the laboratory       12928  2   12 
           system.                                                12928  2   13
